<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:flater.html>flater</a> (28776)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From obsolete <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">flateren</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to chit-chat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:flauwte.html>flauwte</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:flauwte.html>flauwten</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:flauwtes.html>flauwtes</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:flauwte.html>flauwtetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>feebleness, weakness; the quality of lacking strength or vigour</li>
<li>a sudden loss of consciousness; syncope</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">economics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> low demand in markets</li></ol>

***fleck.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fleck.html>fleck</a> (93500)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">flekked</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">flekka</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to spot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*flekk-</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vlek.html>vlek</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fleck.html>fleck</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">flecks</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A flake</li>
<li>A lock, as of wool.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of J. Martin to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A small spot or streak; a speckle.
<ul><li><b>?</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alfred_Tennyson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Alfred Tennyson">Alfred Tennyson</a>, <i>The Talking Oak</i>
<dl><dd>A sunny <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fleck.html>fleck</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fleck.html>fleck</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">flecks</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">flecking</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">flecked</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To mark with small <a href = vnd.unilang:spots.html>spots</a>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1908</b>,  W[illiam] B[lair] M[orton] Ferguson,  chapter IV, in  <cite>Zollenstein</cite>, New York, N.Y. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/D._Appleton_%26_Company" class="extiw" title="w:D. Appleton amp; Company">D. Appleton amp; Company</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/731476803">731476803</a></small>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>So this <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> my future home, I thought!<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>Backed by towering hills, the but faintly discernible purple line of the French boundary off to the southwest, a sky of palest <a href = vnd.unilang:gobelin.html>Gobelin</a> <b>flecked</b> with fat, fleecy little <a href = vnd.unilang:clouds.html>clouds</a>, it in truth looked a dear little city; the city of one's <a href = vnd.unilang:dreams.html>dreams</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***fleur-de-lis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fleur-de-lis.html>fleur-de-lis</a> (49551)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">flower-de-luce</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">flourdelis</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">flour <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> lis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:lily.html>lily</a> flower</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> remodelled after modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:fleur.html>fleur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lys.html>lys</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:lily.html>lily</a> flower</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fleur-de-lis.html>fleur-de-lis</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">fleurs-de-lis</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A design representing a flower whose three petals are joined together at the bottom, often used in heraldry, where it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> particularly associated with the French monarchy.
<ul><li><b>1596</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edmund_Spenser" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Edmund Spenser">Edmund Spenser</a>, <i>The Faerie Queene</i>, V.9:
<dl><dd>Adorned all with gemmes of endlesse price, […] And all embost with Lyons and with <b>Flour-delice</b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2013</b>, Lesley <a href = vnd.unilang:gillian.html>Gillian</a>, <i>The Guardian</i>, 26 Apr 2013:
<dl><dd>One room <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a pink marble bathroom with a gold <a href = vnd.unilang:fleur.html>fleur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lys.html>lys</a> pattern around the tub.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="None" lang="en">⚜</span></li></ul>
</body>

***flikflooien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:flikflooien.html>flikflooien</a> (39583)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:flikken.html>flikken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hit, to flatter, to fix</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vlooien.html>vlooien</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to flatter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:flikflooien.html>flikflooien</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to butter up, flatter hoping for profit in return</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to practice flattery, sycophancy</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to resort to dubious methods or ploys</li></ol>

***flikkeren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:flikkeren.html>flikkeren</a> (27678)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">flickeren</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vlickeren</i>, perhaps equivalent to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vlikken</i>  + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-eren</i>. Perhaps ultimately imitative of <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a>' wings<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>, or from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*flakuraz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shaking, wavering</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, related to <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*flakurōną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to roam, wander</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*plag-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to roam, wander</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pelə-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to wander</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.  Or, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fleuganą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup> 
</p><p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">flikkerje</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">vlickeren</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to beat, flap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">flicorian</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to flap, flutter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">flicker</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">flaunt</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:flikkeren.html>flikkeren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to flicker, to waver unsteadily</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall</li></ol>

***flint.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:flint.html>flint</a> (7916)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">flynt</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:flint.html>flint</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:flint.html>flint</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*flintaz</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vlint</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">flins</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:flint.html>flint</a></i>), from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*splind-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to split, <a href = vnd.unilang:cleave.html>cleave</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Irish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Irish language">Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ga">slinn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slate, shingle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πλίνθος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plínthos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)plei-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to split</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at split.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:flint.html>flint</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:flints.html>flints</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A hard, fine-grained quartz that fractures conchoidally and generates sparks when struck.</li>
<li>A piece of <a href = vnd.unilang:flint.html>flint</a>, such as a gunflint, used to produce a spark.</li>
<li>A small cylinder of some other material of the same function in a cigarette lighter, etc.</li>
<li>A type of maize/corn with a hard outer hull.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Anything figuratively hard.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:flint.html>flint</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:flints.html>flints</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">flinting</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">flinted</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To furnish or decorate an object with <a href = vnd.unilang:flint.html>flint</a>.</li></ol>

***fluit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fluit.html>fluit</a> (5918)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fluit.html>fluit</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fluiten.html>fluiten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fluitje.html>fluitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> flute or the sound it creates</li>
<li>a whistle</li>
<li>organ pipe</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:penis.html>penis</a></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">fluyt</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">flute</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">type of cargo ship</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">fluitschip</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>shortened form of certain compounds, notably fluitglas</li></ol>

<p>See the etymology of the main entry.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">floyten</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fluitketel.html>fluitketel</a> (76000)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fluiten.html>fluiten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to whistle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ketel.html>ketel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">kettle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>A whistling-kettle, which <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> a sharp sound when the boiled water <a href = vnd.unilang:releases.html>releases</a> steam trough a hole on top</li></ol>
